function paru_demo
%PARU_DEMO: test a single sparse matrix in ParU
%
% Usage: paru_demo
%
% See also paru, paru_make, paru_many, paru_tiny, mldivide.

% ParU, Copyright (c) 2022-2024, Mohsen Aznaveh and Timothy A. Davis,
% All Rights Reserved.
% SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0-or-later

type paru_demo
load west0479
A = west0479 ;
n = size (A,1) ;
b = rand (n,1) ;
x = A\b ;
norm (A*x-b)
[x2,paru_stats] = paru (A,b) ;
paru_stats
norm (A*x2-b)


ans =

   2.2006e-10


paru_stats = 

  struct with fields:

     analysis_time: 3.9887e-04
    factorize_time: 0.0018
        solve_time: 6.1035e-05
          strategy: 'unsymmetric'
          ordering: 'colamd(A)'

function paru_demo
%PARU_DEMO: test a single sparse matrix in ParU
%
% Usage: paru_demo
%
% See also paru, paru_make, paru_many, paru_tiny, mldivide.

% ParU, Copyright (c) 2022-2024, Mohsen Aznaveh and Timothy A. Davis,
% All Rights Reserved.
% SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0-or-later

type paru_demo
load west0479
A = west0479 ;
n = size (A,1) ;
b = rand (n,1) ;
x = A\b ;
norm (A*x-b)
[x2,paru_stats] = paru (A,b) ;
paru_stats
norm (A*x2-b)


ans =

   6.4611e-11

ParU control ordering: 1
ParU ordering from UMFPACK: 1

paru_stats = 

  struct with fields:

     analysis_time: 3.9887e-04
    factorize_time: 8.8215e-04
        solve_time: 6.1989e-05
          strategy: 'unsymmetric'
          ordering: 'colamd(A)'


ans =

   2.4805e-09

paru_make 
Compiling ParU for MATLAB.
.........................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................:

function paru_tiny
%PARU_TINY test a tiny sparse matrix with paru
%
% Usage: paru_tiny
%
% See also paru, paru_make, paru_demo, paru_many, mldivide.
%
% ParU, Copyright (c) 2022-2024, Mohsen Aznaveh and Timothy A. Davis,
% All Rights Reserved.
% SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0-or-later

type paru_tiny
A = sparse (rand (2)) ;
b = rand (2,1) ;
x = paru (A,b)
resid = A*x-b

x =

    0.9885
   -0.3400


resid =

   1.0e-15 *

    0.0555
    0.1110
